### [155] [A Note on TurboQuant and the Earlier DRIVE/EDEN Line of Work](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18555)
*Ran Ben-Basat,Yaniv Ben-Itzhak,Gal Mendelson,Michael Mitzenmacher,Amit Portnoy,Shay Vargaftik*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文澄清了TurboQuant与更早的EDEN（含DRIVE）之间的关系，指出TurboQuant的两种变体（TurboQuantₘₛₑ和TurboQuantₚᵣₒd）均为EDEN的特例或次优实现，实验表明EDEN在精度上全面优于TurboQuant。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 澄清TurboQuant与EDEN/DRIVE之间的关系，指出TurboQuant的工作未能正确引用或理解已有方法，并纠正其性能对比中的误导性结论。

Method: 通过理论分析揭示TurboQuantₘₛₑ是EDEN在S=1时的特例（次优），TurboQuantₚᵣₒd则是EDEN的劣化组合（三步次优）；并通过实验验证EDEN（含最优S）在精度上全面超越TurboQuant。

Result: TurboQuantₘₛₑ是EDEN在S=1的次优特例；TurboQuantₚᵣₒd存在三重次优；实验显示EDEN在所有设定下均优于TurboQuant，且有超过1比特的精度优势（如2-bit EDEN优于3-bit TurboQuantₚᵣₒd）。

Conclusion: TurboQuant并未超越EDEN，其声称的贡献实际上是EDEN框架的特例或次优实现，EDEN仍是最优方法。

Abstract: This note clarifies the relationship between the recent TurboQuant work and the earlier DRIVE (NeurIPS 2021) and EDEN (ICML 2022) schemes. DRIVE is a 1-bit quantizer that EDEN extended to any $b>0$ bits per coordinate; we refer to them collectively as EDEN.
  First, TurboQuant$_{\text{mse}}$ is a special case of EDEN obtained by fixing EDEN's scalar scale parameter to $S=1$. EDEN supports both biased and unbiased quantization, each optimized by a different $S$ (chosen via methods described in the EDEN works). The fixed choice $S=1$ used by TurboQuant is generally suboptimal, although the optimal $S$ for biased EDEN converges to $1$ as the dimension grows; accordingly TurboQuant$_{\text{mse}}$ approaches EDEN's behavior for large $d$.
  Second, TurboQuant$_{\text{prod}}$ combines a biased $(b-1)$-bit EDEN step with an unbiased 1-bit QJL quantization of the residual. It is suboptimal in three ways: (1) its $(b-1)$-bit step uses the suboptimal $S=1$; (2) its 1-bit unbiased residual quantization has worse MSE than (unbiased) 1-bit EDEN; (3) chaining a biased $(b-1)$-bit step with a 1-bit unbiased residual step is inferior to unbiasedly quantizing the input directly with $b$-bit EDEN.
  Third, some of the analysis in the TurboQuant work mirrors that of the EDEN works: both exploit the connection between random rotations and the shifted Beta distribution, use the Lloyd-Max algorithm, and note that Randomized Hadamard Transforms can replace uniform random rotations.
  Experiments support these claims: biased EDEN (with optimized $S$) is more accurate than TurboQuant$_{\text{mse}}$, and unbiased EDEN is markedly more accurate than TurboQuant$_{\text{prod}}$, often by more than a bit (e.g., 2-bit EDEN beats 3-bit TurboQuant$_{\text{prod}}$). We also repeat all accuracy experiments from the TurboQuant paper, showing that EDEN outperforms it in every setup we have tried.

</details>


### [156] [Structure-Preserving Gaussian Processes Via Discrete Euler-Lagrange Equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06246)
*Jan-Hendrik Ewering,Kathrin Flaßkamp,Niklas Wahlström,Thomas B. Schön,Thomas Seel*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出拉格朗日高斯过程（LGPs），通过离散受迫欧拉-拉格朗日方程实现概率性、数据高效的动力学学习。该方法在无外力时保持拉格朗日-达朗贝尔原理的几何结构，从而学习物理一致的模型，避免系统能量漂移，实现稳定的长期预测。核心创新在于利用离散受迫欧拉-拉格朗日方程和变分离散化方案构建高斯过程条件化的线性算子，使方法能够仅从离散位置快照（无需速度或动量）学习动力学。在合成数据、真实案例及具有迟滞效应的软体机器人实验中，LGPs展示了数据效率和泛化能力，仅凭稀疏位置数据即可学习物理一致的动力学并进行不确定性量化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有动力学学习方法通常需要速度或动量信息，但在实际场景（如运动捕捉、视觉伺服）中往往只能获取位置测量数据。同时，缺乏几何结构约束的模型会出现能量漂移，导致长期预测不稳定。因此，需要一种既能仅利用位置数据、又能保持物理一致性的概率性学习方法。

Method: 基于离散受迫欧拉-拉格朗日方程和变分离散化方案，构造高斯过程条件化的线性算子，从而在无外力时自动保持拉格朗日-达朗贝尔原理的几何结构。该方法无需速度或动量信息，仅需离散位置快照即可学习系统动力学。

Result: 在合成数据、真实世界案例以及具有迟滞效应的软体机器人实验中，LGPs仅凭稀疏位置数据即可学习物理一致的动力学，提供不确定性量化，并实现稳定的长期预测，展现出数据效率和良好的泛化能力。

Conclusion: 拉格朗日高斯过程（LGPs）是一种有效的概率性动力学学习方法，能够在仅提供稀疏位置数据的情况下，通过学习保持物理一致性的模型，克服能量漂移问题，实现长期稳定的预测。

Abstract: In this paper, we propose Lagrangian Gaussian Processes (LGPs) for probabilistic and data-efficient learning of dynamics via discrete forced Euler-Lagrange equations. Importantly, the geometric structure of the Lagrange-d'Alembert principle, which governs the motion of dynamical systems, is preserved by construction in the absence of external forces. This allows learning physically consistent models that overcome erroneous drift in the system's energy, thereby providing stable long-term predictions. At the core of our approach lie linear operators for Gaussian process conditioning, constructed from discrete forced Euler-Lagrange equations and variational discretization schemes. Thereby and unlike prior work, the method enables learning dynamics from discrete position snapshots, i.e., without access to a system's velocities or momenta. This is particularly relevant for a large class of practical scenarios where only position measurements are available, for instance, in motion capture or visual servoing applications. We demonstrate the data-efficiency and generalization capabilities of the LGPs in various synthetic and real-world case studies, including a real-world soft robot with hysteresis. The experimental results underscore that the LGPs learn physically consistent dynamics with uncertainty quantification solely from sparse positional data and enable stable long-term predictions.

Abstract: Understanding how deep neural networks learn representations remains a central challenge in machine learning theory. In this work, we propose a feature-centric framework for analyzing neural network training by relating weight updates to feature evolution. We introduce a simple identity, the Feature Learning Equation, which identifies the weight Gram matrix as the key object capturing feature dynamics. This enables us to interpret gradient descent as implicitly inducing a hypothetical evolution of features, whose covariance structure - termed the Virtual Covariance - characterizes how representations evolve during training. Building on this perspective, we introduce Target Linearity, a measure quantifying the linear alignment between features and targets. By analyzing the training and layer-wise dynamics, we show that deep networks learn to sequentially transform representations toward target-linear structure. This linearization perspective provides a unified interpretation of several empirical phenomena, including Neural Collapse and linear interpolation in generative models.

### [159] [Trade-off Functions for DP-SGD with Subsampling based on Random Shuffling: Tight Upper and Lower Bounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06259)
*Marten van Dijk,Murat Bilgehan Ertan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文在f-DP框架下对基于随机洗牌子采样的DP-SGD进行了紧致分析，推导出闭式可解析的隐私权衡函数。通过Berry-Esseen定理得到紧致常数界，并证明在σ≥√(3/ln M)时，单轮训练可达到接近理想随机猜测对角线的隐私保证。进一步引入推广的大数定律新证明技术，得到渐近随机猜测对角线极限结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有针对DP-SGD的f-DP分析主要集中在泊松子采样上，虽然可机器计算但缺乏透明性和可解释性。随机洗牌子采样作为一种更实际的子采样方式，其紧致f-DP分析尚未得到充分研究。本文旨在填补这一空白，提供透明、可解析的闭式隐私界。

Method: 在f-DP框架下分析随机洗牌子采样的DP-SGD，利用Berry-Esseen定理推导紧致的闭式隐私权衡函数上界。进一步引入基于推广大数定律的新证明技术，分析多轮次组合下的渐近行为。

Result: 得到闭式的、可解析的隐私权衡函数界，证明在σ≥√(3/ln M)时可达有效隐私保证。单轮场景下给出了具体参数设置（δ=1/100, σ=1时，M≈1.14×10^6轮，N≈1.14×10^7样本）。多轮组合下δ呈线性依赖，限制了E=O(√M)。渐近分析表明若E=c_M²M且c_M→0，组合后的权衡函数一致收敛到1-a，δ仅O(√E)依赖。

Conclusion: 随机洗牌子采样在f-DP框架下可得到比泊松子采样更透明且紧致的隐私分析结果。本文建立的分析框架为实际部署DP-SGD提供了可操作的隐私参数指导，同时指出了精确收敛速率的刻画作为开放问题。

Abstract: We derive a tight analysis of the trade-off function for Differentially Private Stochastic Gradient Descent (DP-SGD) with subsampling based on random shuffling within the $f$-DP framework. Our analysis covers the regime $σ\geq \sqrt{3/\ln M}$, where $σ$ is the noise multiplier and $M$ is the number of rounds within a single epoch. Unlike $f$-DP analyses for Poisson subsampling, which yield non-closed implicit formulas that can be machine computed but are non-transparent, random shuffling admits a tight analysis yielding transparent and interpretable closed-form bounds. Our concrete bounds, derived via the Berry-Esseen theorem, are tight up to constant factors within the proof framework. We demonstrate worked parameter settings for a single epoch ($E=1$) with a corresponding trade-off function $\geq 1-a-δ$, that is, only $δ$ below the ideal random guessing diagonal $1-a$: For $δ= 1/100$ and $σ= 1$, roughly $M \approx 1.14\times 10^6$ rounds and $N \approx 1.14\times 10^7$ training samples suffice to achieve meaningful differential privacy. This is in contrast to recent negative results for the regime $σ\leq 1/\sqrt{2 \ln M}$. Our concrete bounds can be composed over multiple epochs leading to $δ$ having a linear in $E$ dependency, which restricts $E=O(\sqrt{M})$. To go beyond Berry--Esseen, we introduce a new proof technique based on a generalization of the law of large numbers that yields an asymptotic random guessing diagonal-limit result: if $E=c_M^2M$ with $c_M\to 0$, then the $E$-fold composed trade-off function satisfies $f^{\otimes E}(a)\to 1-a$ uniformly in $a\in[0,1]$ with $δ$ having only an $O(\sqrt{E})$ dependency. We compare this asymptotic regime with the corresponding Poisson subsampling asymptotic, and highlight the characterization of explicit convergence rates as an open question.

### [160] [Beyond Rigid Alignment: Graph Federated Learning via Dual Manifold Calibration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06260)
*Wentao Yu,Bo Han,Jie Yang,Chen Gong*

TL;DR: 本文提出FedGMC，一种从流形统一视角解决图联邦学习中语义与结构异质性的新范式。通过双流形校准机制（语义流形+结构流形），在保留全局共性的同时最大化局部个性化表示空间，在11个数据集上显著超越现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图联邦学习方法通过强制对齐模型参数或原型来应对异质性，这隐式依赖于全局线性假设，用一个全局一致的表征空间压缩了客户端的个性化表示空间，无法保留多样的局部图分布。

Method: 提出FedGMC双流形校准机制：1）针对语义异质性，服务端通过等距语义锚构建几何最优的语义流形，指导局部语义流形校准；2）针对结构异质性，服务端通过全局结构模板构建全局结构流形，指导局部结构流形校准；3）服务端聚合局部流形动态优化全局语义流形和结构流形。

Result: 在11个同配性和异配性图数据集上的大量实验表明，FedGMC有效平衡了全局共性和局部个性化，显著优于当前最先进的基线方法。

Conclusion: 从流形视角统一处理语义和结构异质性，通过柔性校准而非强制对齐，能更好地保留个性化表示空间，实现全局与局部信息的有效平衡。

Abstract: Graph Federated Learning (GFL) enables collaborative representation learning across distributed subgraphs while preserving privacy. However, heterogeneity remains a critical challenge, as subgraphs across clients typically differ significantly in both semantics and structures. Existing methods address heterogeneity by enforcing the rigid alignment of model parameters or prototypes between clients and the server. However, these alignments implicitly rely on a restrictive global linearity assumption that summarizes local data distributions using a single and globally consistent representation space. This severely compresses the personalized representation space of clients and fails to preserve diverse local graph distributions. To overcome these limitations, we propose Federated Graph Manifold Calibration (FedGMC), a novel paradigm that tackles semantic heterogeneity and structural heterogeneity from a unified manifold perspective. Instead of enforcing rigid alignment, FedGMC introduces a dual manifold calibration mechanism that preserves global commonalities while maximizing the personalized representation space of local clients. Specifically, for semantic heterogeneity, the server constructs a geometrically optimal semantic manifold via equidistant semantic anchors, so as to guide the calibration of local semantic manifolds. For structural heterogeneity, the server constructs a global structural manifold by building global structural templates, so as to guide the calibration of local structural manifolds. Finally, the server dynamically refines both global semantic manifolds and structural manifolds by aggregating local manifolds. Extensive experiments on eleven homophilic and heterophilic graphs demonstrate that FedGMC effectively balances global commonality and local personalization, thereby significantly outperforming state-of-the-art baseline methods.

</details>


### [161] [Inference-Time Refinement Closes the Synthetic-Real Gap in Tabular Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06261)
*Eugenio Lomurno,Filippo Balzarini,Francesco Benelle,Francesca Pia Panaccione,Matteo Matteucci*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出TARDIS，一种在推理阶段对预训练扩散骨干模型进行细化的框架，通过双向Chamfer精炼策略在15个表格数据基准上超越真实数据效用（中位+8.6%），且无需重新训练模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前扩散模型生成的合成表格数据在效用上接近但难以超越真实数据，此前改进仅局限于训练阶段（架构优化、缩放、重新训练），推理阶段的细化方法几乎未被探索。

Method: TARDIS框架包含三个组件：(1) 推理时采样细化，通过Tree-structured Parzen Estimator搜索分数级引导参数；(2) 双向Chamfer精炼（BCR），对称最小化合成样本与真实样本之间的Chamfer距离，包括连续分数级梯度优化和离散批排序后处理；(3) 可选软标签蒸馏步骤。整个流程在冻结的预训练扩散骨干上操作。

Result: 在15个二分类、多分类和回归基准上，TARDIS达到中位+8.6%的下游任务提升（超过真实数据训练模型），95%置信区间[+3.3, +16.4]，Wilcoxon p=0.016，11/15严格胜出；在所有15个数据集上优于TabDiff骨干（平均+12.9%，p<10^-4）；在流形保真度、多样性和样本级隐私方面与骨干持平；推理时间1-80分钟（单消费级GPU）。

Conclusion: 推理时细化预训练表格扩散骨干可以在不重新训练的情况下达到并超越真实数据效用，BCR被验证为跨数据集的主导细化模式，为合成表格数据生成提供了训练时方法之外的互补路径。

Abstract: Diffusion-based generators set the current state of the art for synthetic tabular data. These methods approach but rarely exceed real-data utility, and closing this synthetic-real gap has so far been pursued exclusively at training time, via architectural advances, scaling, and retraining of monolithic generators. The inference-time alternative, i.e., refining the outputs of a pre-trained backbone with parameters left untouched, has remained largely unexplored for tabular synthesis. We introduce TARDIS (Tabular generation through Refinement, Distillation, and Inference-time Sampling), an inference-time refinement framework that operates on a frozen pre-trained backbone, configured per dataset by a Tree-structured Parzen Estimator search over score-level guidance during reverse diffusion, with each trial's objective set by an inner grid search over post-hoc sample selectors and an optional soft-label distillation step. The search space encodes a single mathematical pattern we name Bidirectional Chamfer Refinement (BCR): the symmetric Chamfer functional between synthetic and real samples is minimized both continuously, via a score-level gradient, and discretely, via batch-ranking post-generation. The per-dataset search recovers BCR-aligned configurations on most datasets, evidence for BCR as the dominant refinement pattern. Across 15 binary, multiclass, and regression benchmarks TARDIS achieves a median +8.6% downstream-task improvement over models trained on real data (95% CI [+3.3, +16.4], Wilcoxon p=0.016, 11/15 strict wins) and improves over the TabDiff backbone on all 15 datasets (mean +12.9%, p<10^-4), matching the backbone on manifold fidelity, diversity, and sample-level privacy. Inference-time refinement of a pre-trained tabular diffusion backbone reaches and exceeds real-data utility in 1 to 80 minutes on a single consumer-grade GPU.

### [162] [Can Attribution Predict Risk? From Multi-View Attribution to Planning Risk Signals in End-to-End Autonomous Driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06264)
*Le Yang,Ruoyu Chen,Haijun Liu,Jiawei Liang,ShangQuan Sun,Xiaochun Cao*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种面向端到端自动驾驶规划的分层归因框架，通过由粗到精的区域归因策略从六视图输入中定位关键视觉证据，并提取三种归因统计量（熵、空间方差、基尼系数）作为规划风险的预测信号。实验表明这些统计量与轨迹误差和碰撞检测具有显著相关性，并且具有良好的泛化性和稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有端到端自动驾驶模型虽然提升了系统集成度，但存在决策不透明、风险难以定位的问题。已有的辅助监控模型或文本解释方法脱离规划过程本身，无法揭示轨迹生成背后的视觉证据。归因方法虽可直接解释模型，但规划任务与图像分类不同，需处理六视角连续多步轨迹预测，要求捕捉关键视角和区域及其对输出的影响，且归因图能否支持风险识别尚不明确。

Method: 提出分层归因框架：1) 以与原始轨迹的L2一致性为优化目标，设计由粗到精的区域归因策略，先在六视图全空间搜索候选区域，再在候选区域内精细化归因；2) 提取三种归因统计量作为风险预测信号：归因熵（衡量注意力集中程度）、相机内空间方差（表征视角内分布分散度）、跨相机基尼系数（量化六相机间分布不均匀性）。

Result: 在BridgeAD、UniAD和GenAD三个模型上，所提统计量与轨迹误差的Spearman相关系数达到0.30±0.07，碰撞检测的AUROC达到0.77±0.04。该信号可泛化到未见场景且性能下降可忽略，并在替代归因基线下保持稳定。

Conclusion: 所提出的分层归因框架能有效揭示端到端规划模型的视觉证据，且提取的归因统计量可作为规划风险的可靠预测信号，具有良好的泛化性和鲁棒性，为自动驾驶规划的可解释性和安全性分析提供了新途径。

Abstract: End-to-end autonomous driving models generate future trajectories from multi-view inputs, improving system integration but introducing opaque decisions and hard-to-localize risks. Existing methods either rely on auxiliary monitoring models or generate textual explanations, but are decoupled from the planning process and fail to reveal the visual evidence underlying trajectory generation. While attribution offers a direct alternative, planning differs from image classification by taking six-view camera images as input and predicting continuous multi-step trajectories, requiring attribution to capture both critical views and regions and their influence on outputs. Moreover, whether attribution maps can support risk identification remains underexplored. To address this, we propose a hierarchical attribution framework for end-to-end planning. Specifically, using L2 consistency with the original trajectory as the objective, we design a coarse-to-fine region attribution strategy that searches candidate regions across the full six-view input and refines attribution within them. We further extract three attribution statistics as predictive signals for planning risk, including attribution entropy to measure how concentrated the planner's reliance is over the joint visual space, within-camera spatial variance to characterize how spread out the attribution is within each view, and cross-camera Gini coefficient to quantify how unevenly attribution is distributed across the six cameras. Experiments on BridgeAD, UniAD, and GenAD show that these statistics correlate with planning risk, achieving Spearman correlations of $0.30 \pm 0.07$ with trajectory error and AUROC of $0.77 \pm 0.04$ for collision detection. The signal generalizes to held-out scenes with negligible degradation and remains stable under an alternative attribution baseline.

Abstract: While generative modeling has achieved remarkable success on tasks like natural language-conditioned image generation, enabling model adaptation from example data points remains a relatively underexplored and challenging problem. To this end, we propose Function Projection for Flow Matching (FP-FM), an algorithm that directly conditions generation on samples from the target distribution. FP-FM learns basis functions to span the velocity fields corresponding to a set of training distributions, and adapts to new distributions by computing a simple least-squares projection onto this basis. This enables efficient generation of samples from diverse target distributions without additional training at inference time. Method: HACE包含两个组件：(1) 预测聚合：将模型概率质量沿层次结构向上传播，使父节点累积子节点的置信度；(2) 祖先标签平滑：将真实标签信号沿从叶节点到根节点的路径进行分布，而非仅作用于单一类别。

Abstract: Standard cross-entropy is the default classification loss across virtually all of machine learning, yet it treats all misclassifications equally, ignoring the semantic distances that a class hierarchy encodes. We propose Hierarchy-Aware Cross-Entropy (HACE), a drop-in replacement for standard cross-entropy that incorporates a known class hierarchy directly into the loss. HACE combines two components: prediction aggregation, which propagates the model's probability mass upward through the class hierarchy to ensure that parent nodes accumulate the confidence of their children; and ancestral label smoothing, which distributes the ground-truth signal along the path from the true class to the root. We evaluate HACE on CIFAR-100, FGVC Aircraft, and NABirds in two regimes: end-to-end training across six architectures spanning convolutional and attention-based designs, and linear probing on frozen DINOv2-Large features. In end-to-end training, HACE improves accuracy over standard cross-entropy in 15 out of 18 architecture--dataset pairs, with a mean gain of 4.66\%. Method: INEUS采用无网格迭代框架，核心创新是用单跳采样替代非局部跳跃积分的显式求值，将PIDE求解重构为一系列递归回归问题。该方法在全局时空域上学习解，避免了计算完整PIDE残差的昂贵微分过程。

Conclusion: INEUS是一种高效、可扩展的高维PIDE求解方法，通过巧妙设计避免了非局部项的计算瓶颈，兼顾了收敛性保证与计算效率。

Abstract: In this paper, we introduce INEUS, a meshfree iterative neural solver for partial integro-differential equations (PIDEs). The method replaces the explicit evaluation of nonlocal jump integrals with single-jump sampling and reformulates PIDE solving as a sequence of recursive regression problems. Like Physics-Informed Neural Networks (PINNs), INEUS learns global solutions over the entire space-time domain, yet it offers a more efficient treatment of nonlocal terms and avoids the computationally expensive differentiation of full PIDE residuals. These features make INEUS particularly well suited for high-dimensional PDEs and PIDEs. Supported by a contraction-based convergence proof for linear PIDEs, our numerical experiments show that INEUS delivers accurate and scalable solutions for various high-dimensional linear and nonlinear examples.

Our theory provides a sufficient condition under which bringing neuron switching surfaces sufficiently close to data points ensures their intersection with local neighborhoods, which in turn implies a strict increase in the local affine-region count, yielding a principled training-time handle for seeding data-relevant partitions early in optimization. Guided by these results, we propose a plug-and-play region-seeding regularizer that encourages early partitioning while allowing task-driven refinement to dominate later in training. Motivation: 现有深度时序预测模型虽规模庞大，但使用固定的共享权重矩阵处理所有时间token，导致静态模式响应——模型只能学习到次优的平均动态，无法适应时变局部模式。

Method: 提出DPR（动态模式重校准）机制，包含三个步骤：1）感知：提取token级特征；2）路由：对一组学习到的自适应响应模式基计算软路由分布；3）调制：生成时变调制向量，通过残差Hadamard积重校准隐藏状态。该机制是骨干网络无关的适配器，也可作为独立模型DPRNet。

Result: DPR作为适配器显著提升了多种现有架构的预测性能；作为独立模型DPRNet在12个时序预测基准上取得了具有竞争力的结果。

Conclusion: 动态重校准相比宏观参数扩展是一种更有效的改进方向，证明了自适应token级动态处理是时序预测中的通用瓶颈。

Abstract: Local temporal patterns in real-world time series continuously shift, rendering globally shared transformations suboptimal. Current deep forecasting models, despite their scale and complexity, rely on fixed weight matrices applied uniformly to all temporal tokens. This creates a static pattern response: models settle into a compromised average, unable to adapt to changing local dynamics. We introduce Dynamic Pattern Recalibration (DPR), a backbone-agnostic mechanism that resolves this via token-level recalibration. Through a lightweight "Perceive-Route-Modulate" pipeline, DPR computes a soft-routing distribution over a learned basis of adaptive response patterns, generating a time-aware modulation vector that recalibrates hidden states via a residual Hadamard product. As a backbone-agnostic adapter, DPR enhances forecasting across diverse architectures with minimal overhead, confirming it addresses a general bottleneck. As a minimalist standalone model, DPRNet achieves competitive performance across 12 benchmarks, validating dynamic recalibration against macroscopic parameter scaling.

### [169] [When Does $\ell_2$-Boosting Overfit Benignly? High-Dimensional Risk Asymptotics and the $\ell_1$ Implicit Bias](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06314)
*Ye Su,Jian Li,Yong Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了贪婪集成方法（特别是ℓ₂-Boosting）在高维线性回归中的良性过拟合现象，发现ℓ₁隐式偏差会导致噪声局部化，使得过拟合风险以对数速率衰减（而非ℓ₂几何中的线性速率），并提出了一种基于子梯度动力学的早停规则，可恢复Lasso基本不等式并达到极小极大最优预测率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 良性过拟合在ℓ₂几何中已被充分刻画，但在受ℓ₁隐式偏差驱动的贪婪集成方法（如Boosting）中，其行为因坐标选择阈值的非线性耦合而难以分析。现有谱解析工具失效，亟需新的理论框架来理解这类算法的高维风险特征。

Method: 将凸高斯极小极大定理与双截断高斯矩的渐近展开相结合，解析地处理非光滑ℓ₁插值问题；利用子梯度动力学分析Boosting流的非光滑微分包含，推导早停规则。

Result: 在纯噪声各向同性模型下，贪婪选择的噪声局部化导致过拟合风险以对数速率Θ(σ²/log(p/n))衰减，而非线性速率。在尖峰-各向同性设计中，当尾维度r₂ ≫ n时风险趋于零，但速率为Θ(σ²/log(r₂/n))，慢于ℓ₂几何。早停规则在ℓ₁路径有界条件下恢复Lasso基本不等式，达到极小极大最优预测率。

Conclusion: ℓ₁隐式偏差会导致噪声局部化和更慢的对数衰减率，这是贪婪集成方法区别于ℓ₂正则化方法的特有现象；通过子梯度动力学设计的早停规则可有效规避这一慢速收敛问题。

Abstract: Benign overfitting is well-characterized in $\ell_2$ geometries, but its behavior under the $\ell_1$ implicit bias of greedy ensembles remains challenging. The analytical barrier stems from the non-linear coupling of coordinate selection thresholds, which invalidates standard spectral resolvent tools. To isolate this algorithmic bias, we characterize the high-dimensional risk of continuous-time $\ell_2$-Boosting over $p$ features and $n$ samples. By coupling the Convex Gaussian Minimax Theorem with delicate asymptotic expansions of double-sided truncated Gaussian moments, we analytically resolve the non-smooth $\ell_1$ interpolant. Under an isotropic pure-noise model, we prove that benign overfitting fails at the linear rate: greedy selection localizes noise into sparse active sets, and the excess variance decays at a logarithmic rate $Θ(σ^2/\log(p/n))$ for noise variance $σ^2$. We remark that while this localization mechanism should persist in the presence of signals, the exact signal-noise decomposition remains an open problem. For spiked-isotropic designs with $k^*$ head eigenvalues and $r_2 = p - k^*$ tail dimensions, the risk converges to zero when $r_{2} \gg n$, but only at a logarithmic rate $Θ(σ^2/\log(r_2/n))$, which is slower than the linear decay observed in $\ell_2$ geometries. To avoid this slow convergence, we analyze the non-smooth subdifferential dynamics of the boosting flow. This yields a tuning-free early stopping rule that, under a bounded $\ell_1$-path condition, recovers the Lasso basic inequality and attains the minimax-optimal empirical prediction rate for $\ell_1$-bounded signals.

### [170] [Pro-KLShampoo: Projected KL-Shampoo with Whitening Recovered by Orthogonalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06316)
*Ruotong Sun,Ermin Wei*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Pro-KLShampoo利用KL-Shampoo预条件子的"尖峰-平坦"特征谱结构，通过追踪低维子空间的全谱信息并对剩余方向施加正交化，在多个规模上比KL-Shampoo更节省内存、更快收敛且验证损失更低。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM预训练中，显式Kronecker分解预条件（如KL-Shampoo）与梯度动量正交化（如Muon）两条路线独立发展，作者观察到KL-Shampoo的Kronecker因子具有尖峰-平坦特征值谱结构，希望利用这一结构将两类方法结合以实现更高效的优化器。

Method: 作者提出Pro-KLShampoo：将KL-Shampoo的一个Kronecker因子限制为参数化族——在追踪的r维子空间保留完整谱结构，在剩余n-r维方向上共享单一特征值并对该方向施加正交化，理论上证明该正交化恢复完整KL-Shampoo预条件子的代数形式。

Result: 在GPT-2 124M/350M和LLaMA 134M/450M四个规模上，Pro-KLShampoo在所有测试的子空间秩下，验证损失、每GPU峰值内存和达到各损失水平的墙钟时间均一致优于KL-Shampoo。

Conclusion: 利用预条件子的结构化特征谱并结合正交化，可以在不牺牲收敛质量的前提下显著降低Kronecker优化器的计算与存储开销，为LLM预训练优化器提供了一条统一Kronecker方法和正交化方法的新路径。

Abstract: Optimizers that exploit the matrix structure of gradients are central to modern LLM pre-training, with two distinct frontiers: explicit Kronecker-factored preconditioning -- most recently KL-Shampoo, which estimates the preconditioner via KL divergence minimization -- and orthogonalization of the gradient momentum, exemplified by Muon and analyzed as steepest descent under the spectral norm. The two routes are typically developed in isolation. We make a structural observation about KL-Shampoo's Kronecker preconditioners: their eigenvalue spectra exhibit a \emph{spike-and-flat} shape -- a few dominant eigenvalues followed by an approximately uniform tail -- across layers and training stages, holding exactly under a rank-$ρ$ signal-plus-noise gradient model. We exploit this structure by restricting one of KL-Shampoo's Kronecker factors to a parametric family aligned with the spike-and-flat shape: full spectral structure on a tracked $r$-dimensional subspace, single shared eigenvalue across the remaining $n-r$ directions. On these directions, we apply orthogonalization. An identity shows that this orthogonalization recovers the algebraic form of full KL-Shampoo's preconditioner. On four pre-training scales (GPT-2 124M / 350M, LLaMA 134M / 450M), Pro-KLShampoo consistently outperforms KL-Shampoo at every subspace rank we test in validation loss, peak per-GPU memory, and wallclock time to reach each loss level.

Method: 采用权重共享的Transformer（53K参数），通过多次前向传播（passes）迭代生成SMILES。使用错误分类、线性探针和稀疏自编码器分析模型内部表征，并通过系统消融实验定位关键注意力头。

Abstract: Language models for molecular design have scaled to hundreds of millions of parameters, yet how they learn chemical grammar is poorly understood. We train SMolLM, a 53K-parameter weight-shared transformer, to generate novel SMILES with 95% validity on the ZINC-250K drug-like-molecule benchmark, outperforming a standard GPT with 10 times more parameters. Mechanistically, the same block resolves SMILES constraints across passes in a fixed order: brackets first, rings second, and valence last, as shown by error classification, linear probing, and sparse autoencoders. A systematic ablation across attention heads and passes further localizes the first bracket-matching step to a single attention head. Together, these results yield a compact, mechanistically interpretable molecular generator and a testbed for studying iterative computation in formal-language domains.

### [172] [LINC: Decoupling Local Consequence Scoring from Hidden Matching in Constructive Neural Routing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06332)
*Shaofeng Qin,Li Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了LINC（局部推理通过归一化比较），一种解码器端候选决策架构，通过显式计算动作的局部确定性后果（如行驶、等待、时间松弛、容量变化），并使用共享线性局部评分器比较这些中心化的相对后果，同时用可行集摘要调制解码器上下文，从而减轻隐藏状态重新发现转移算术的负担。在CVRPTW、CVRP和TSP上均取得显著改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有构造性神经路由求解器通常通过匹配解码器上下文与候选嵌入来评分下一个动作，隐藏了行驶、等待、松弛和容量变化等确定性的单步后果，导致模型需要从隐藏状态中重新学习这些转移算术，效率低下。

Method: 提出LINC架构：1) 显式计算每个候选动作的局部确定性后果（时间、容量等）；2) 将这些后果按决策角色使用——中心化的相对后果通过共享线性局部评分器进行比较；3) 可行集摘要用于调制解码器上下文；4) 同时保留标准全局匹配机制。

Result: 在CVRPTW上，LINC将PolyNet的Solomon/Homberger gaps从13.83%/38.15%降至7.26%/14.71%；在TSP和CVRP上也改进了外部基准的gaps。

Conclusion: 显式建模确定性单步后果能有效提升神经路由求解器的性能，LINC架构为受约束的路径规划问题提供了一种简洁有效的解码器改进方案。

Abstract: Constructive neural routing solvers usually score the next action by matching a decoder context to candidate embeddings, hiding deterministic one-step consequences such as travel, waiting, slack, and capacity changes. We propose LINC (Local Inference via Normed Comparison), a decoder-side candidate decision architecture that computes these consequences explicitly. LINC uses them according to their decision role: centered relative consequences are compared by a shared linear local scorer, while feasible-set summaries modulate the decoder context. This preserves standard global matching and relieves the hidden state from rediscovering transition arithmetic. The Capacitated Vehicle Routing Problem with Time Windows (CVRPTW) serves as the main constrained-routing stress test; the same interface extends to the Capacitated Vehicle Routing Problem (CVRP) and Traveling Salesman Problem (TSP). In particular, for CVRPTW, LINC reduces PolyNet's Solomon/Homberger gaps from 13.83\%/38.15\% to 7.26\%/14.71\%; for TSP and CVRP, it also improves external-benchmark gaps.

### [173] [Eliciting associations between clinical variables from LLMs via comparison questions across populations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06335)
*Fabian Kabus,Kian Kordtomeikel,Thomas Brox,Heinz Wiendl,Daiana Stolz,Harald Binder*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于三元组比较问题的间接 elicitation 方法，从 LLM 中恢复患者特征间的相关性和因果结构，并通过提示级环境偏移实现不变因果预测（ICP），在 COPD 和 MS 两个临床领域验证了方法的有效性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出基于患者比较三元组问题的结构化比较方法，结合无需访问模型激活值或内部表示的统计模型。通过引入第二变量信息观察 LLM 相似性决策的变化，并利用提示级环境偏移获得不同子群体的相关估计，最终采用不变因果预测（ICP）获得保守的候选父节点因果链接。

Result: 在 COPD 和 MS 两个临床领域中，不同提示环境下 elicitation 得到的相关估计平滑、稳定且具有临床可解释性，同时在统计上存在显著差异，支持下游的不变性检验。ICP 能够提供少量候选的不变父节点因果链接。

Abstract: The training data of large language models (LLMs) comprises a wide range of biomedical literature, reflecting data from many different patient populations. We investigate how it might be possible to recover information on correlation and causal links between patient characteristics, as a key building block for medical decision making. To avoid the pitfalls of direct elicitation, we propose an approach based on structured comparison questions, specifically patient comparison triplet questions. This is combined with a statistical model for the LLM representation that provides estimates of correlations without access to activations or model internals. Intuitively, we consider how similarity decisions of LLMs based on a first variable are affected by providing information on a second variable for one of the patients being assessed. We then induce prompt-level environment shifts to obtain correlation estimates for different subpopulations, which enables an invariant causal prediction (ICP) approach to obtain conservative candidate parent links. We demonstrate the method in two clinical domains, chronic obstructive pulmonary disease (COPD) and multiple sclerosis (MS). Across prompted environments, the elicited correlations are smooth, stable, and clinically interpretable, yet vary in a statistically significant way that supports downstream invariance testing, such that ICP provides a small set of candidate invariant parent links. These results show that indirect elicitation via triplet comparisons can recover meaningful association structure from LLMs and offer a cautious route from implicit correlations to causal statements that are congruent with LLM answering patterns.

### [174] [Is Escalation Worth It? A Decision-Theoretic Characterization of LLM Cascades](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06350)
*Dylan Bouchard*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个基于约束优化和对偶理论的模型级联决策框架，揭示了成本-质量前沿的几何特性（分段凹性、对偶影子价格），并通过五个基准测试、八种模型的实验验证了：确定性阈值级联中，两模型两两组合的包络线优于完整固定链；轻量级预生成路由器因避免了廉价模型的生成成本而优于最佳级联策略，表明级联性能主要受结构性成本（级联在 escalation 前必须先支付廉价模型成本）限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有模型级联方法将延迟阈值视为经验超参数，缺乏对成本-质量前沿几何特性的理论指导，且对模型池中多模型组合的优化策略理解不足。

Method: 1. 基于约束优化和对偶理论建立决策框架；2. 证明两模型级联成本-质量前沿的逐段凹性及对偶影子价格互易关系；3. 将 k 模型确定性两模型阈值级联的前沿刻画为 C(k,2) 个两两级联的逐点包络；4. 推导 k 模型级联的一阶条件（单一影子价格均衡跨阶段的边际质量-成本比）；5. 在五个基准、八模型上进行实验验证。

Result: 1. 确定性阈值级联类中，完整固定链不如两两组合包络线；2. 优化子序列级联无实际有意义的增益；3. 轻量级预生成路由器在四个数据集上优于最佳级联策略，主要因其避免了将查询直接发送给大模型时廉价模型的生成成本，而非路由信号更强。

Conclusion: 级联性能主要受结构性成本限制（级联在 escalation 前必须支付廉价模型成本），而非中间阶段不足；改进方向应聚焦于减少结构性成本。

Abstract: Model cascades, in which a cheap LLM defers to an expensive one on low-confidence queries, are widely used to navigate the cost-quality tradeoff at deployment. Existing approaches largely treat the deferral threshold as an empirical hyperparameter, with limited guidance on the geometry of the resulting cost-quality frontier over a model pool. We develop a decision-theoretic framework grounded in constrained optimization and duality. For a two-model cascade, we establish piecewise concavity of the cost-quality frontier on decreasing-benefit regions of the confidence support, with reciprocal shadow prices linking the budget- and quality-constrained formulations. Given a pool of $k$ models, we characterize the frontier achievable by deterministic two-model threshold cascades as the pointwise envelope over $\binom{k}{2}$ pairwise cascades, with switching points where the optimal pair changes. For $k$-model cascades, we derive first-order conditions in which a single shadow price equalizes marginal quality-per-cost across stage boundaries. We validate the framework on five benchmarks (MATH, MMLU, TriviaQA, SimpleQA, LiveCodeBench) across eight models from five providers. Within the deterministic threshold-cascade class, full fixed chains underperform the pairwise envelope, and optimized subsequence cascades do not deliver practically meaningful held-out gains over it. A lightweight pre-generation router exceeds the best cascade policy on four of five datasets, mainly because it avoids the cheap model's generation cost on queries sent directly to a larger model rather than because of a stronger routing signal. These results suggest that cascade performance is limited primarily by structural cost, since cascades pay the cheap model before any escalation decision, rather than by a shortage of intermediate stages.

### [175] [Memory Efficient Full-gradient Attacks (MEFA) Framework for Adversarial Defense Evaluations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06357)
*Yuan Du,Mitchel Hill,HanQin Cai*

TL;DR: 本文研究了迭代随机纯化防御在白盒对抗攻击下的鲁棒评估问题。关键洞察是利用梯度检查点技术实现长纯化轨迹的精确端到端梯度计算，从而支持全梯度自适应攻击。相比先前因内存限制而采用近似反向传播的方法，全梯度攻击能发现被遗漏的脆弱点，产生更强的$\ell_{\infty}$和$\ell_{2}$白盒攻击。研究表明，精确梯度评估对于迭代随机防御的可靠基准测试至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有迭代随机纯化防御的鲁棒性评估因内存限制而采用近似反向传播，这会削弱攻击信号并高估模型鲁棒性；同时，迭代过程中的随机性缺乏有效控制，不同纯化轨迹会显著改变报告的鲁棒性指标。

Method: 提出了内存高效的全梯度评估框架，结合梯度检查点反向传播（以额外重计算换取代价更低的内存使用）和控制随机变异性的评估协议，在减少内存瓶颈的同时保留精确梯度。

Result: 在基于扩散的纯化和基于能量模型的Langevin采样上，全梯度攻击发现了近似梯度评估遗漏的脆弱点，产生了更强的$\ell_{\infty}$和$\ell_{2}$白盒攻击，并支持探测分布外鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 精确梯度评估对迭代随机防御的可靠基准测试至关重要。

Abstract: This work studies the robust evaluation of iterative stochastic purification defenses under white-box adversarial attacks. Our key technical insight is that gradient checkpointing makes exact end-to-end gradient computation through long purification trajectories practical by trading additional recomputation for substantially lower memory usage. This enables full-gradient adaptive attacks against diffusion- and Langevin-based purification defenses, where prior evaluations often resort to approximate backpropagation due to memory constraints. These approximations can weaken the attack signal and risk overestimating robustness. In parallel, stochasticity in iterative purification is frequently under-controlled, even though different purification trajectories can substantially change reported robustness metrics. Building on this insight, we introduce a memory-efficient full-gradient evaluation framework for stochastic purification defenses. The framework combines checkpointed backpropagation with evaluation protocols that control stochastic variability, thereby reducing memory bottlenecks while preserving exact gradients. We evaluate diffusion-based purification and Langevin sampling with Energy-Based Models (EBMs), demonstrating that full-gradient attacks uncover vulnerabilities missed by approximate-gradient evaluations. Our framework yields stronger state-of-the-art $\ell_{\infty}$ and $\ell_{2}$ white-box attacks and further supports probing out-of-distribution robustness. Overall, our results show that exact-gradient evaluation is essential for reliable benchmarking of iterative stochastic defenses.

*Alessandro Pagani,Marco Cominelli,Liying Han,Gaofeng Dong,Sergio Benini,Francesco Gringoli,Mattia Savardi,Mani B. Srivastava,Trevor Bihl,Erik P. Blasch,Daniel O. Brigham,Kara Combs,Lance M. Kaplan,Federico Cerutti*

TL;DR: 本文初步分析了Chronos基础模型在处理和内部表示频域信息方面的能力，通过使用轻量级在线最小描述长度探针分析解码器架构，发现该模型能够捕获频率信息，但在某些频段表示质量会下降。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管时间序列基础模型被广泛采用，但它们编码基本信号属性的程度尚未得到充分表征，现有研究缺乏对模型内部频率信息表示的深入理解。

Method: 在受控条件下生成离散正弦信号，使用轻量级在线最小描述长度探针作用于Chronos解码器架构，测试模型内部表示中频率信息的存在性和可分离性。

Result: 模型能够捕获频率信息，但不同频段的表示质量存在差异，某些频段可能出现退化或需要特别关注。

Conclusion: 该研究为信号处理和信息融合场景中Chronos的使用者提供了实践指导，并推动了时间序列基础模型可解释性和评估方面的持续改进。

Abstract: This paper presents a preliminary analysis of the ability of Chronos foundation model to process and internally represent frequency domain information. Foundation models that process time-series data offer practitioners a unified architecture capable of learning generic temporal representations across diverse tasks and domains, reducing the need for task-specific feature engineering and enabling transfer across signal modalities. Despite their growing adoption, the extent to which such models encode fundamental signal properties remains insufficiently characterised. We address this gap by analysing Chronos under controlled conditions, starting from the simplest class of signals: discrete sinusoids generated at fixed frequencies. Using lightweight online minimum description length probes applied to the decoder architecture, we test for the presence and separability of frequency information in the model's internal representations. The results provide insight into how frequential content is captured across the frequency spectrum and highlight regimes in which representation quality may degrade or require particular care. These findings offer practical guidance for users of Chronos in signal processing and information fusion contexts, and contribute to ongoing efforts to improve the interpretability and evaluation of foundation models for temporal data.

### [177] [Flow Matching with Arbitrary Auxiliary Paths](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06364)
*Xin Peng,Ang Gao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出AuxPath-FM框架，通过引入任意分布的辅助变量η来泛化条件流匹配，支持多种先验分布和标签引导生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有条件流匹配方法将辅助分量限制为高斯噪声，缺乏灵活性。AuxPath-FM旨在解除这一限制，允许辅助变量服从任意分布，从而设计更多样化的概率路径。

Method: 通过引入任意分布的辅助变量η，构建形如X_t = a(t)X_1 + b(t)X_0 + c(t)η的轨迹。理论上证明该构造保持连续性方程，并与边际公式的训练目标一致。支持高斯、均匀、拉普拉斯、离散Rademacher等多种先验分布。

Result: 理论证明AuxPath-FM保持连续性方程且训练目标与边际公式一致；不同先验分布展现出独特的几何特性；可编码结构化语义信息实现标签引导生成。

Conclusion: AuxPath-FM为概率路径设计提供了原则性的通用基础，兼具理论通用性和实际灵活性，适用于多种生成建模任务。

Abstract: We introduce a new generative modeling framework, \textbf{Flow Matching with Arbitrary Auxiliary Paths (AuxPath-FM)}, which generalizes conditional flow matching by incorporating an auxiliary variable drawn from an arbitrary distribution into the probability path. Unlike prior methods that restrict auxiliary components to Gaussian noise, AuxPath-FM allows the variable $η$ to follow any distribution, producing trajectories of the form $X_t = a(t)X_1 + b(t)X_0 + c(t)η$. We theoretically demonstrate that this construction preserves the continuity equation and maintains a training objective consistent with the marginal formulation. This flexibility enables the design of diverse probability paths using various priors, including Gaussian, Uniform, Laplace, and discrete Rademacher distributions, each offering unique geometric properties for generative flows. Furthermore, our framework allows for specialized tasks such as label-guided generation by encoding structured semantic information into the auxiliary distribution. Overall, AuxPath-FM provides a principled and general foundation for probability path design, offering both theoretical generality and practical flexibility for diverse generative modeling tasks.

### [178] [Layer Collapse in Diffusion Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06366)
*Alexander Conzelmann,Albert Catalan-Tatjer,Shiwei Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文发现扩散语言模型（LLaDA-8B）存在一种“层坍缩”现象：早期少数层表现出高度相似的激活模式，被一个持续长token范围的大超级离群点主导。该离群点虽看似冗余，但对模型输出至关重要，剪除会导致输出退化为重复随机token循环。与自回归模型相反，DLM中早期层冗余度最高，且层坍缩源于过训练而非欠训练。实际应用方面，DLM对量化压缩高度鲁棒（3-bit GPTQ仅降1.8% vs Llama降64.7%），且最优稀疏性分配策略与AR模型完全相反。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散语言模型（DLM）已成为自回归（AR）语言模型的有力替代方案，但两者在激活动态上的差异尚不明确。本文旨在系统刻画DLM的激活特性，理解其层动力学与AR模型的根本区别，并探索这些差异对模型压缩和部署的实际影响。

Method: 以LLaDA-8B为研究对象，通过分析激活模式识别层坍缩现象；采用离群点剪除实验验证其重要性；使用GPTQ量化评估压缩鲁棒性；通过稀疏性分配策略对比DLM与AR模型（Llama-3.1-8B）的最优配置差异；并辅以受控预训练实验验证层坍缩成因。

Result: 发现DLM早期层存在被超级离群点主导的坍缩激活模式，该离群点不可或缺；DLM整体冗余度更高且早期层最冗余（与AR模型相反）；层坍缩源于过训练而非欠训练；DLM对3-bit量化高度鲁棒（GSM8K仅降1.8% vs Llama-64.7%）；最优稀疏分配策略在两类模型中完全相反。

Conclusion: DLM的训练目标从根本上重塑了层动力学，使其与AR模型产生本质差异。这些发现对模型压缩和实际部署具有直接指导意义：DLM更适合激进量化，且应采用与AR模型相反的稀疏化策略。

Abstract: Diffusion language models (DLMs) have recently emerged as competitive alternatives to autoregressive (AR) language models, yet differences in their activation dynamics remain poorly understood. We characterize these dynamics in LLaDA-8B and identify a striking layer-collapse property: a few early layers exhibit highly similar, collapsed activation patterns dominated by a single large super-outlier persisting over a long token range. Despite its apparent redundancy, this outlier is critical: pruning it causes outputs to degrade into repetitive random token loops. Paradoxically, layers in LLaDA contain more redundant representations overall, with redundancy most pronounced in earlier layers -- the reverse of AR models, where deeper layers grow redundant due to undertraining. Our analysis indicates that layer collapse in DLMs is not driven by undertraining but by overtraining: a dominant outlier becomes an indispensable information carrier while remaining representations collapse into redundant structure. These findings have strong practical implications, verified through controlled pre-training experiments. DLMs are surprisingly robust to compression: LLaDA under 3-bit GPTQ quantization drops only -1.8% on GSM8K, whereas Llama-3.1-8B drops -64.7%. Optimal sparsity allocation also reverses between families: at 50% average sparsity, allocating more to early layers in LLaDA yields +8.4% over the reverse strategy, while the same allocation costs Llama -8.4%. Our findings reveal that the DLM training objective fundamentally reshapes layer dynamics relative to AR models, with direct consequences for compression and deployment. Code: github.com/Conzel/super-outlier-dlm.

</details>


### [179] [A Unified Pair-GRPO Family: From Implicit to Explicit Preference Constraints for Stable and General RL Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06375)
*Hao Yu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出Pair-GRPO家族（含Soft-Pair-GRPO和Hard-Pair-GRPO），通过二元偏好奖励替代分组归一化标量奖励，解决了RLHF中策略更新不稳定、梯度方向模糊、可解释性差和高梯度方差等问题。理论证明Soft-Pair-GRPO梯度是标准GRPO的正标量倍数，Hard-Pair-GRPO进一步引入局部概率约束和约束KL拟合优化。实验表明在LLM对齐和连续控制任务上优于现有基线。

Method: 提出Pair-GRPO家族，包含两个变体：(1) Soft-Pair-GRPO：将GRPO的分组归一化标量奖励替换为二元成对偏好奖励，保留裁剪代理和KL正则化结构；(2) Hard-Pair-GRPO：引入显式局部概率约束和约束KL拟合优化，进一步抑制梯度噪声和全局策略漂移。理论层面证明了梯度等价定理、单调策略改进、确定性梯度方向、梯度方差缩减和动态步长收敛性。

Result: 在HH-RLHF、UltraFeedback等LLM对齐基准和MuJoCo HalfCheetah-v4连续控制任务上，Pair-GRPO家族在对齐质量、人类偏好胜率、训练稳定性和泛化能力方面一致优于SOTA基线。消融实验验证了各核心组件的关键贡献。

Conclusion: Pair-GRPO家族通过理论驱动的设计，系统解决了偏好学习中多个核心问题，并在多个任务上验证了其有效性和泛化能力，为偏好强化学习提供了统一的理论框架和实用算法。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) alignment via reinforcement learning from human preferences (RLHF) suffers from unstable policy updates, ambiguous gradient directions, poor interpretability, and high gradient variance in mainstream pairwise preference learning paradigms. To systematically address these limitations, we establish a unified theoretical framework for preference-based RL optimization centered on the Pair-GRPO family, comprising two tightly coupled variants: Soft-Pair-GRPO and Hard-Pair-GRPO. Soft-Pair-GRPO is a minimal modification of Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) that replaces group-normalized scalar rewards with binary pairwise preference rewards, retaining GRPO's clipped surrogate and KL-regularized structure. We prove a critical gradient equivalence theorem: under first-order Taylor expansion around the current policy, Soft-Pair-GRPO's gradient is a positive scalar multiple of standard GRPO's gradient, explaining its empirical stability despite discarding continuous reward magnitudes. Building on this foundation, we propose Hard-Pair-GRPO, an advanced variant introducing explicit local probability constraints and constrained KL-fitting optimization to further suppress gradient noise and global policy drift. We provide comprehensive theoretical guarantees for both variants--including monotonic policy improvement, deterministic gradient direction, gradient-variance reduction, and dynamic step-size convergence. Extensive experiments on standard LLM alignment benchmarks (HH-RLHF,UltraFeedback) and the MuJoCo continuous control task HalfCheetah-v4 demonstrate that our Pair-GRPO family consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines in alignment quality, human preference win rate, training stability, and generalization to general reinforcement learning. Ablation studies validate the critical contributions of each core component.

### [180] [MinMax Recurrent Neural Cascades](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06384)
*Alessandro Ronca*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出基于MinMax代数的递归神经网络级联（RNCs），该模型不受梯度爆炸/消失影响，具备正则语言表达能力、对数级并行计算能力，并在理论和实践中展现出优于传统RNN的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统RNN（如LSTM、GRU）存在梯度消失/爆炸问题，限制了其处理长序列和深层结构的能力。作者希望找到一种既具有强表达能力，又能避免梯度问题的递归形式。

Method: 利用MinMax代数（最小值与最大值运算）定义一种新型递归形式，将多层神经元级联构成MinMax RNCs。该模型状态和激活值在整个输入长度上一致有界，梯度几乎处处存在且有界，且状态关于过去状态的梯度可恒为1。

Result: 理论上：可表达所有正则语言（有限记忆系统的最大表达能力）；并行评估时间复杂度为O(log n)；状态与激活值一致有界；梯度几乎处处存在且有界；无状态梯度消失问题。实验上：在多个合成任务中完美求解，优于现有SOTA RNN；训练了1.27亿参数的MinMax RNC进行下一个token预测，在其规模下表现出竞争力的性能。

Conclusion: MinMax RNCs在理论上兼具强表达力、高效计算和梯度稳定性，实践上也展现出优越性能，具有替代传统RNN的潜力。

Abstract: We show that the MinMax algebra provides a form of recurrence that is expressively powerful, efficiently implementable, and most importantly it is not affected by vanishing or exploding gradient. We call MinMax Recurrent Neural Cascades (RNCs) the models obtained by cascading several layers of neurons that employ such recurrence. We show that MinMax RNCs enjoy many favourable theoretical properties. First, their formal expressivity includes all regular languages, arguably the maximal expressivity for a finite-memory system. Second, they can be evaluated in parallel with a runtime that is logarithmic in the input length given enough processors; and they can also be evaluated sequentially. Third, their state and activations are bounded uniformly for all input lengths. Fourth, at almost all points, their loss gradient exists and it is bounded. Fifth, they do not exhibit a vanishing state gradient: the gradient of a state w.r.t. a past state can have constant value one regardless of the time distance between the two states. Finally, we find empirical evidence that the favourable theoretical properties of MinMax RNCs are matched by their practical capabilities: they are able to perfectly solve a number of synthetic tasks, showing superior performance compared to the considered state-of-the-art recurrent neural networks; also, we train a MinMax RNC of 127M parameters on next-token prediction, and the obtained model shows competitive performance for its size, providing evidence of the potential of MinMax RNCs on real-world tasks.

Abstract: On-policy distillation (OPD) trains a student on its own trajectories with token-level teacher feedback and often outperforms off-policy distillation and standard reinforcement learning. ### [183] [Consistent Geometric Deep Learning via Hilbert Bundles and Cellular Sheaves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06395)
*Kartik Tandon,Julian Gould,Tanishq Bhatia,Francesca Dominici,Alejandro Ribeiro,Claudio Battiloro*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出HilbNets框架，将卷积学习推广到流形上无限维信号（如时间序列、概率分布、算子），通过希尔伯特丛上的连接拉普拉斯算子定义卷积，并利用两步采样策略实现可计算性：先是流形采样得到希尔伯特细胞层（推广图结构），再对信号离散化，证明了从离散到连续的收敛性和跨采样迁移性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代深度学习架构越来越多地处理本征无限维信号（如时间序列、概率分布、算子），且定义在不规则域上，但缺乏统一的学习理论。现有几何学习方法（如图拉普拉斯）仅能处理有限维标量信号，无法直接处理每个点上具有独立希尔伯特空间的信号场景。

Method: (1) 利用希尔伯特丛上的连接拉普拉斯作为卷积算子，定义滤波器和神经网络HilbNets；(2) 两步采样策略：首先流形采样诱导希尔伯特细胞层（推广图结构，特征空间为希尔伯特空间，边带耦合规则），证明其层拉普拉斯在概率意义下收敛到底层连接拉普拉斯（Belkin & Niyogi收敛定理的无穷维丛推广）；其次对信号离散化，证明离散HilbNets收敛到连续架构且跨采样迁移。

Result: 理论上建立了无限维信号上卷积学习的统一框架，证明了层拉普拉斯到连接拉普拉斯的收敛性以及离散HilbNets到连续架构的收敛性与迁移性；实验上在合成任务和真实任务上验证了框架的有效性。

Conclusion: 该工作将经典拉普拉斯几何学习框架提升到每个点信号位于自身希尔伯特空间的场景，拓宽了几何学习的整体范围，为处理无限维信号提供了理论基础和可实现的算法框架。

Abstract: Modern deep learning architectures increasingly contend with sophisticated signals that are natively infinite-dimensional, such as time series, probability distributions, or operators, and are defined over irregular domains. Yet, a unified learning theory for these settings has been lacking. To start addressing this gap, we introduce a novel convolutional learning framework for possibly infinite-dimensional signals supported on a manifold. Namely, we use the connection Laplacian associated with a Hilbert bundle as a convolutional operator, and we derive filters and neural networks, dubbed as \textit{HilbNets}. We make HilbNets and, more generally, the convolution operation, implementable via a two-stage sampling procedure. First, we show that sampling the manifold induces a Hilbert Cellular Sheaf, a generalized graph structure with Hilbert feature spaces and edge-wise coupling rules, and we prove that its sheaf Laplacian converges in probability to the underlying connection Laplacian as the sampling density increases. Notably, this result is a generalization to the infinite-dimensional bundle setting of the Belkin \& Niyogi \cite{BELKIN20081289} convergence result for the graph Laplacian to the manifold Laplacian, a theoretical cornerstone of geometric learning methods. Second, we discretize the signals and prove that the discretized (implementable) HilbNets converge to the underlying continuous architectures and are transferable across different samplings of the same bundle, providing consistency for learning. Finally, we validate our framework on synthetic and real-world tasks. Overall, our results broaden the scope of geometric learning as a whole by lifting classical Laplacian-based frameworks to settings where the signal at each point lives in its own Hilbert space.

*Liu Hanzuo,Chaofan Lin,Weixuan Sun,Yulong Wang,Key,Rayying,Mingyu Gao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SparseForge是一种半结构化剪枝后训练框架，通过直接优化稀疏掩码而非增加重训练数据量，在2:4稀疏度下用5B token使LLaMA-2-7B达到57.27%零样本准确率，超越稠密模型并接近需40B token的最优方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 半结构化剪枝后质量下降严重，现有方法依赖大规模稀疏重训练来恢复精度，计算成本高昂。

Method: 结合Hessian感知的重要性估计与软掩码逐步退火为硬件可执行的半结构化稀疏模式，直接优化稀疏掩码。

Result: 在LLaMA-2-7B的2:4稀疏度下，仅用5B重训练token即达57.27%零样本准确率，超过稠密模型的56.43%，接近SOTA方法40B token的57.52%。该精度-效率权衡优势在多个模型家族上一致。

Conclusion: SparseForge通过直接优化掩码显著提升了半结构化剪枝后恢复的效率与效果，实现了更优的精度-效率权衡。

Abstract: Semi-structured sparsity provides a practical path to accelerate large language models (LLMs) with native hardware support, but post-training semi-structured pruning often suffers from substantial quality degradation due to strong structural coupling. Existing methods rely on large-scale sparse retraining to recover accuracy, resulting in high computational cost.
  We propose SparseForge, a post-training framework that improves recovery efficiency by directly optimizing the sparsity mask rather than scaling up retraining tokens. SparseForge combines Hessian-aware importance estimation with progressive annealing of soft masks into hardware-executable structured sparsity, enabling stable and efficient sparse recovery. On LLaMA-2-7B under 2:4 sparsity, SparseForge achieves 57.27% average zero-shot accuracy with only $\textbf{5B}$ retraining tokens, surpassing the dense model's 56.43% accuracy and approaching the 57.52% result of a state-of-the-art method using $\textbf{40B}$ tokens. Such improvements on the accuracy-efficiency trade-off from SparseForge are shown to be consistent across model families.

</details>


### [185] [FRInGe: Distribution-Space Integrated Gradients with Fisher--Rao Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06404)
*Gabriele Martino,Sebastian Tschiatschek*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出 Fisher-Rao Integrated Gradients (FRInGe)，通过在预测分布空间而非输入空间定义参考点和插值路径，解决了 Integrated Gradients 因启发式基线、直线路径、离散化和饱和导致的脆弱性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于梯度的归因方法（如 Integrated Gradients）虽然模型忠实且可扩展，但依赖于启发式基线、直线积分路径、离散化近似以及饱和区域，导致解释结果不稳定且不可靠。

Method: FRInGe 在预测分布空间（概率单纯形）中选择最大熵预测作为参考点，并沿 Fisher-Rao 测地线定义插值路径；通过 pullback Fisher 度量将路径映射回输入空间，利用 KL 散度和欧几里得信任域稳定路径，最终沿此轨迹对输入梯度积分得到归因。

Result: 在六种 ImageNet 架构上，FRInGe 在面向校准的归因指标上提升最为显著（尤其是 MAS 分数），同时在扰动 AUC 和不忠实度指标上保持竞争力。

Conclusion: FRInGe 通过将归因路径从输入空间迁移到预测分布空间，提供了一种更稳定、更符合概率几何结构的归因计算方法，有效缓解了传统 Integrated Gradients 的固有问题。

Abstract: Gradient-based attribution methods are model-faithful and scalable, but Integrated Gradients (IG) can be brittle because explanations depend on heuristic baselines, straight-line paths, discretization, and saturation. We propose Fisher--Rao Integrated Gradients (FRInGe), which defines both the reference and interpolation schedule in predictive distribution space. FRInGe replaces input baselines with a maximum-entropy predictive reference and follows a Fisher-Rao geodesic on the probability simplex. The corresponding input-space trajectory is realized through the pullback Fisher metric and stabilized by KL and Euclidean trust regions; attributions are obtained by integrating input gradients along this trajectory. Across six ImageNet architectures, FRInGe most clearly improves calibration-oriented attribution metrics, especially MAS scores, while remaining competitive on perturbation AUC and infidelity.

</details>


### [186] [E = T*H/(O+B): A Dimensionless Control Parameter for Mixture-of-Experts Ecology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06415)
*Qingjun Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一个无量纲控制参数 E = T*H/(O+B)，用于预测混合专家模型（MoE）是否会形成健康的专家生态或出现专家死亡现象。通过12项控制实验，证明 E >= 0.5 足以保证零死亡专家，无需手工设计的负载均衡辅助损失函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MoE模型训练中专家死亡（dead experts）问题严重，传统依赖手工设计的负载均衡辅助损失函数来缓解，缺乏统一的诊断框架。本文旨在提出一个简洁的控制参数来预测和调控专家生态健康。

Method: 提出无量纲参数 E = T*H/(O+B)，其中T为路由温度，H为路由熵权重，O为专家oracle权重，B为平衡权重。在8个视觉任务和4个语言任务上进行了12项控制实验，总计超过11,000个训练epoch，在CIFAR-10、CIFAR-100、TinyImageNet-200、WikiText-2和WikiText-103上验证。

Result: E >= 0.5 足以保证零死亡专家。还发现六个额外结果：死亡专家可复苏、正交毒性具有数据集依赖性、任务复杂度改变临界E阈值、模型过拟合与专家生态健康解耦、三层MoE自发坍塌为两层、生态结构在50倍温度范围内保持不变。

Conclusion: E可作为MoE训练的统一直诊工具，类比于流体力学中的雷诺数。该参数简化了MoE训练中的负载均衡问题，消除了对手工辅助损失的依赖。

Abstract: We introduce E = T*H/(O+B), a dimensionless control parameter that predicts whether Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) models will develop a healthy expert ecology or collapse into dead experts. E combines four hyperparameters -- routing temperature T, routing entropy weight H, oracle weight O, and balance weight B -- into a single quantity. Through 12 controlled experiments (8 vision, 4 language) totaling over 11,000 training epochs, we establish that E >= 0.5 alone is sufficient to guarantee zero dead experts, removing the necessity for handcrafted load-balancing auxiliary losses. We validate this cross-modally on CIFAR-10, CIFAR-100, TinyImageNet-200, WikiText-2, and WikiText-103. Six additional findings emerge: (1) dead experts can resuscitate -- triggered by balance loss driving router re-exploration; (2) ortho toxicity is dataset-dependent, not universal; (3) task complexity shifts the critical E threshold; (4) model overfitting is decoupled from expert ecological health; (5) three-tier MoE spontaneously collapses into a two-tier functional structure; (6) ecological structure is temperature-invariant across a 50x range. We propose that E serves as a unified diagnostic for MoE training, analogous to the Reynolds number in fluid dynamics.

</details>


### [187] [Federated Cross-Client Subgraph Pattern Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06433)
*Selin Ceydeli,Rui Wang,Kubilay Atasu*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于GNN的子图模式检测方法假设图数据集中存储，但在分布式多参与方场景中，客户端本地GNN计算与集中式模型存在表示等价性差距。本文将其形式化为结构可观测性问题，即跨分区的子图模式在局部不可识别。

Method: 提出逐层嵌入交换框架，客户端在前向传播的每一层同步中间节点表示，不暴露原始特征或标签。基于扩展子图假设和跨客户端的共享模型参数，该框架能够恢复与全图集中式GNN相同的节点表示。嵌入交换采用每步新鲜而非每周期陈旧的同步策略。

Result: 在包含环、双团和散聚模式的合成有向多重图上的实验表明，嵌入交换与联邦参数聚合是互补而非可互换的，两者结合可恢复大部分表示差距，前提是交换的嵌入是每步新鲜而非每周期陈旧。

Conclusion: 本文验证了分布式GNN子图模式检测中，逐层嵌入交换与联邦聚合的互补性，为跨分区图上的GNN部署提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Subgraph pattern detection aims to uncover complex interaction structures in graphs. However, state-of-the-art graph neural network (GNN)-based solutions assume centralized access to the entire graph. When graphs are instead distributed across multiple parties, client-local GNN computations diverge from those of a centralized model, resulting in a representation-equivalence gap. We formalize this as a structural observability problem, where subgraph patterns crossing partition boundaries become locally unidentifiable. To bridge this gap, we propose a per-step, layer-wise embedding exchange framework in which clients synchronize intermediate node representations at each layer of the forward pass, without exposing raw features or labels. Under an extended-subgraph assumption and shared model parameters across clients, this framework recovers the same node representations as a centralized GNN over the full graph. Experiments on synthetic directed multigraphs with cycles, bicliques, and scatter-gather patterns show that embedding exchange and federated parameter aggregation are complementary rather than interchangeable: their combination recovers most of the representation gap, provided exchanged embeddings are fresh per-step rather than stale per-epoch.

### [188] [Hyperbolic Concept Bottleneck Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06440)
*Daniel Uyterlinde,Swasti Shreya Mishra,Pascal Mettes*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有概念瓶颈模型将概念嵌入平坦欧氏空间，视为独立正交维度，忽略了概念本身具有的层次结构和语义组织关系，导致模型与真实概念结构不匹配。

Method: 在双曲空间中利用蕴含锥（entailment cones）的几何包含关系定义概念激活信号（包含边界内的裕度），无需额外监督或学习模块即可产生稀疏、层次感知的激活；并提出自适应缩放法则，实现沿概念树层次一致地传播用户干预。

Result: 在稀疏数据场景下，HypCBM性能与使用20倍数据的后验欧氏模型相当；具有更强的层次一致性和对输入损坏的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 双曲几何为概念瓶颈模型提供了更自然的归纳偏置，能够在保持可解释性的同时提升稀疏数据下的效率和鲁棒性。

Abstract: Concept Bottleneck Models (CBMs) have become a popular approach to enable interpretability in neural networks by constraining classifier inputs to a set of human-understandable concepts. While effective, current models embed concepts in flat Euclidean space, treating them as independent, orthogonal dimensions. Concepts, however, are highly structured and organized in semantic hierarchies. To resolve this mismatch, we propose Hyperbolic Concept Bottleneck Models (HypCBM), a post-hoc framework that grounds the bottleneck in this structure by reformulating concept activation as asymmetric geometric containment in hyperbolic space. Rather than treating entailment cones as a pre-training penalty, we show they encode a natural test-time activation signal: the margin of inclusion within a concept's entailment cone yields sparse, hierarchy-aware activations without any additional supervision or learned modules. We further introduce an adaptive scaling law for hierarchically faithful interventions, propagating user corrections coherently through the concept tree. Empirically, HypCBM rivals post-hoc Euclidean models trained on 20$\times$ more data in sparse regimes required for human interpretability, with stronger hierarchical consistency and improved robustness to input corruptions.

### [189] [FedFrozen: Two-Stage Federated Optimization via Attention Kernel Freezing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06446)
*Junye Du,Zhenghao Li,Yushi Feng,Long Feng*

Main category: cs.LG

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有联邦优化方法通常通过目标级正则化或更新校正机制解决客户端漂移问题，而近期研究表明Transformer架构在异构联邦训练中可能比传统模型更具鲁棒性。受此启发，本文探究注意力机制中不同参数组件如何影响联邦优化，旨在提出一种更有效的异构联邦学习优化框架。

Method: 将注意力模块分解为查询/键块（决定注意力核）和值块（在诱导核下进行语义变换），提出FedFrozen两阶段框架：第一阶段全模型预热训练，第二阶段冻结查询/键块、仅优化值块。在线性注意力公式下进行理论分析，将预热阶段解释为正则化核轮廓目标的不精确下降过程，冻结阶段简化为固定注意力核下的受限优化问题。

Result: 仿真实验验证了预测的偏置-漂移行为，真实数据实验表明FedFrozen在异构联邦学习中提升了Transformer模型的稳定性和有效性，并揭示了预热长度的显式权衡关系。

Conclusion: 本文通过分解注意力机制中的不同参数组件，提出FedFrozen框架有效缓解了异构联邦学习中的客户端漂移问题，理论分析和实验验证了该方法的优势，为Transformer在联邦学习中的应用提供了新的优化范式。

Abstract: Federated learning with heterogeneous clients remains a significant challenge for deep learning, primarily due to client drift arising from inconsistent local updates. Existing federated optimization methods typically address this issue through objective-level regularization or update-correction mechanisms. Recent studies, however, suggest that Transformer-based architectures may be inherently more robust than conventional models under heterogeneous federated training. Motivated by this observation, we investigate how different parameter components within the attention mechanism influence federated optimization. Specifically, we decompose the attention module into a query/key block, which determines the attention kernel, and a value block, which performs semantic transformation under the induced kernel. Based on this perspective, we propose FedFrozen, a two-stage federated optimization framework that first performs full-model warm-up training and then freezes the query/key block while continuing to optimize the value block. Under a linear-attention formulation, we show that the warm-up stage can be interpreted as an inexact descent procedure on a regularized kernel-profile objective, while the frozen stage reduces to a restricted value-block optimization problem under a fixed attention kernel. Our analysis further reveals an explicit trade-off that governs the choice of warm-up length. Simulations validate the predicted bias-drift behavior, and real-data experiments demonstrate that FedFrozen improves both the stability and effectiveness of Transformer models in heterogeneous federated learning.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 贝叶斯优化在代理模型和采集函数正确指定时，有限样本蒙特卡洛误差会扰动采集值，导致候选排名翻转和次优决策。这一被忽视的失败模式需要有效的方差缩减方法。

Method: 提出正交采集估计器，通过减去最优加权得分函数控制变量，使采集残差与后验得分方向正交，从而降低蒙特卡洛方差。结合集成代理模型和外部对数变换，形成OrthoBO框架。

Abstract: Bayesian optimization is widely used for hyperparameter optimization when model evaluations are expensive; however, noisy acquisition estimates can lead to unstable decisions. We identify acquisition estimation noise as a failure mode that was previously overlooked: even when the surrogate model and acquisition target are correctly specified, finite-sample Monte Carlo error can perturb acquisition values. This can, in turn, flip candidate rankings and lead to suboptimal BO decisions. As a remedy, we aim at variance reduction and propose an orthogonal acquisition estimator that subtracts an optimally weighted score-function control variate, which yields an acquisition residual orthogonal to posterior score directions and which thus reduces Monte Carlo variance. We further introduce OrthoBO: a Bayesian optimization framework that combines our orthogonal acquisition estimator with ensemble surrogates and an outer log transformation. We show theoretically that our estimator preserves the target, leads to variance reduction, and improves pairwise ranking stability. We further verify the theoretical properties of OrthoBO through numerical experiments where our framework reduces acquisition estimation variance, stabilizes candidate rankings, and achieves strong performance. We also demonstrate the downstream utility of OrthoBO in hyperparameter optimization for neural network training and fine-tuning.

### [192] [Invariant Features in Language Models: Geometric Characterization and Model Attribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06458)
*Agnibh Dasgupta,Abdullah Tanvir,Xin Zhong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种局部几何框架，将语义不变性解释为语言模型潜在空间中沿干扰方向变化、在不变子空间中保持语义身份的结构化区域。通过对比性子空间发现方法，分离语义改变与语义保持的变异，并应用于零样本模型归因。实验表明不变结构出现在特定深度区域，语义位移多位于干扰子空间之外，不变成分对模型输出有因果作用，且能捕获模型特定几何模式用于准确归因。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: (1) 提出局部几何框架，将语义等价输入映射到潜在空间中的结构化区域，其中释义变化沿干扰方向分布，语义身份由不变子空间保持；(2) 设计对比性子空间发现方法，分离语义改变与语义保持的变异；(3) 将不变表示应用于零样本模型归因任务。

Result: 不变结构在特定深度区域涌现；语义位移大部分位于干扰子空间之外；表示层面的干预证明不变成分对模型输出具有因果作用；不变表示捕获了模型特定的几何模式，实现了准确的模型归因。

Conclusion: 语义不变性可被视为语言模型潜在表示的一种局部几何属性，为理解语言模型如何组织意义提供了原则性视角。

Abstract: Language models exhibit strong robustness to paraphrasing, suggesting that semantic information may be encoded through stable internal representations, yet the structure and origin of such invariance remain unclear. We propose a local geometric framework in which semantically equivalent inputs occupy structured regions in latent space, with paraphrastic variation along nuisance directions and semantic identity preserved in invariant subspaces. Building on this view, we make three contributions: (1) a geometric characterization of invariant latent features, (2) a contrastive subspace discovery method that separates semantic-changing from semantic-preserving variation, and (3) an application of invariant representations to zero-shot model attribution. Across models and layers, empirical results support these contributions. Invariant structure emerges in specific depth regions, semantic displacement lies largely outside the nuisance subspace, and representation-level interventions indicate a causal role of invariant components in model outputs. Invariant representations also capture model-specific geometric patterns, enabling accurate attribution. These findings suggest that semantic invariance can be viewed as a local geometric property of latent representations, offering a principled perspective on how language models organize meaning.

### [193] [MINER: Mining Multimodal Internal Representation for Efficient Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06460)
*Weien Li,Rui Song,Zeyu Li,Haochen Liu,Gonghao Zhang,Difan Jiao,Zhenwei Tang,Bowei He,Haolun Wu,Xue Liu,Ye Yuan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出MINER，一种轻量级插件模块，通过探测和融合Transformer内部层的检索相关信息，生成单一紧凑嵌入，在不牺牲单向量检索效率的前提下，显著提升视觉文档检索质量，最高比基线提升4.5% nDCG@5，并将与晚期交互检索的差距缩小至0.2。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: MINER包含两个阶段：1) 检索对齐的层探测（Retrieval-Aligned Layer Probing），在每层附加轻量探针，识别携带检索相关信息的维度；2) 自适应稀疏多层融合（Adaptive Sparse Multi-Layer Fusion），对选定层应用性能自适应的神经元级掩码，将幸存信号融合为最终密集向量。

Result: 在ViDoRe V1/V2/V3基准上，MINER在多数评测中优于现有密集单向量检索器，相对对应骨干网络最高提升4.5% nDCG@5；在某些设置下，与强晚期交互基线相比，将nDCG@5差距缩小至0.2。

Conclusion: MINER作为一种轻量插件模块，能够在不修改骨干网络且不牺牲密集检索存储与速度优势的前提下，有效融合内部层信号，显著提升视觉文档单向量检索的质量，缩小与晚期交互方法的差距。

Abstract: Visual document retrieval has become essential for accessing information in visually rich documents. Existing approaches fall into two camps. Late-interaction retrievers achieve strong quality through fine-grained token-level matching but store hundreds of vectors per page, incurring large index footprints and high serving costs. By contrast, dense single-vector retrievers retain storage and latency advantages but consistently lag in quality because they compress all information into a single final-layer embedding. In this work, we first conduct a layerwise diagnostic on single-vector retrievers, revealing that retrieval-relevant signal resides in internal representations. Motivated by these findings, we propose MINER (Mining Multimodal Internal RepreseNtation for Efficient Retrieval), a lightweight plug-in module that probes and fuses internal signals across transformer layers into a single compact embedding without modifying the backbone or sacrificing single-vector efficiency. The first Retrieval-Aligned Layer Probing stage attaches a lightweight probe at each layer, surfacing which dimensions carry retrieval-relevant information. The subsequent Adaptive Sparse Multi-Layer Fusion stage applies performance-adaptive neuron-level masking to the selected layers and fuses the surviving signals into the final dense vector. Across ViDoRe V1/V2/V3, MINER outperforms existing dense single-vector retrievers on the majority of benchmarks, with up to 4.5% nDCG@5 improvement over its corresponding backbone. Compared to strong late-interaction baselines, in some settings MINER substantially narrows the nDCG@$5$ gap to $0.2$ while preserving the storage and serving advantages of dense retrieval.

*Richard von Moos,Mathieu Alain,Bastian Rieck*

Main category: cs.LG

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 不变量比标准GNN更具表达能力；不变量有效表征了结构异质性；不变量能预测多任务性能；基于不变量的非训练模型在26个数据集上能与Transformer和消息传递模型竞争甚至超越。

Conclusion: 表达能力不是预测性能的主要驱动因素；在结构重要的任务上，非可训练的结构代理通常能匹配可训练的消息传递模型。不变量基线应成为评估任务是否需要结构信息以及模型是否捕获了结构信息的标准，为图基础模型的构建奠定基础。

Abstract: Progress on graph foundation models is hindered by benchmark practices that conflate the contributions of node features and graph structure, making it hard to tell whether a model actually learns from connectivity, or whether it even needs to. We propose addressing this using graph invariants, i.e., permutation-invariant, task-agnostic structural descriptors that serve as a diagnostic framework for graph benchmarks. We show that (i) invariants are more expressive than standard GNNs, (ii) invariants characterize structural heterogeneity within and across benchmark datasets, (iii) invariants predict multi-task performance, and (iv) simple invariant-based models are competitive with, and sometimes exceed, transformer and message-passing baselines across 26 datasets. Our results suggest that expressivity is not the main driver of predictive performance, and that on tasks where structure matters, a non-trainable structural proxy often matches trained message-passing models. We thus posit that invariant baselines should become a standard for evaluating whether structure is required for a task and whether a model picks up on it, serving as a stepping stone towards graph foundation models.

Our work addresses these issues by tracking the structural diversity of a graph across coarsening levels. The resulting graph embeddings, which we denote diversity curves, are interpretable by construction, efficient, and directly comparable across coarsening hierarchies. Specifically, we track the spread of graphs, a novel isometry invariant that is inherently well-suited for encoding the metric diversity and geometry of graphs. We utilise edge contraction coarsening and prove that this improves expressivity, thus leading to more powerful graph-level representations than structural descriptors alone. Demonstrating their utility over a range of baseline methods in practice, we use diversity curves to (i) cluster and visualise simulated graphs across varying sizes, (ii) distinguish the geometry of single-cell graphs, (iii) compare the structure of molecular graph datasets, and (iv) characterise geometric shapes.

### [197] [Hitting Time Isomorphism for Multi-Stage Planning with Foundation Policies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06470)
*Magnus Victor Boock,Abdullah Akgül,Mustafa Mert Çelikok,Melih Kandemir*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的算子理论表示学习框架，用于离线强化学习，通过击中时间观测恢复受控马尔可夫过程的定向时间几何。基于该理论，提出了同构嵌入学习（IEL）算法，该算法结合了HILP风格的一致性目标和显式击中时间回归，学习到的非对称、组合式几何结构支持基于图的多阶段长程导航规划。实验证明IEL在离线迷宫导航数据上达到了最先进的策略学习性能。

Method: 提出算子理论表示学习框架，在潜在线性闭包假设下证明表示存在且唯一（至多相差有界线性同构）。推导有限维下击中时间全局误差由单步转移误差和瞬态谱半径决定。在此基础上设计IEL算法，使用HILP风格一致性目标和显式击中时间回归损失联合优化。

Result: 理论方面：给出了有限样本保证，包括近似误差、统计复杂度和轨迹标签不匹配分析。实验方面：在离线迷宫导航数据上IEL方法超越了现有最优基础策略学习算法。

Abstract: We present a new operator-theoretic representation learning framework for offline reinforcement learning that recovers the directed temporal geometry of a controlled Markov process from hitting time observations. While prior art often produces symmetric distances or fails to satisfy the triangle inequality, our framework learns a Hilbert-space displacement geometry where expected hitting times are realized as linear functionals of latent displacements. We prove that this representation exists under latent linear closure and is uniquely identifiable up to a bounded linear isomorphism. For finite-dimensional implementations, we show that global hitting-time error is bounded by one-step transition error amplified by the environment's transient spectral radius. Furthermore, we provide finite-sample guarantees accounting for approximation, statistical complexity, and trajectory-label mismatch. Derived from this theory, we curate Isomorphic Embedding Learning (IEL) as a new goal-agnostic foundation policy learning algorithm that anchors a HILP-style consistency objective with explicit hitting-time regression to ensure that the learned geometry reflects actual decision-time progress. This asymmetric and compositional structure enables robust graph-based multi-stage planning for long-horizon navigation. Our experiments demonstrate that IEL improves the state of the art of learning foundation policy policies from offline maze locomotion data. Our code can be found on https://github.com/MagnusBoock/IEL

### [198] [Efficient Serving for Dynamic Agent Workflows with Prediction-based KV-Cache Management](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06472)
*Haoyu Zheng,Fangcheng Fu,Jia Wu,Binhang Yuan,Yongqiang Zhang,Hao Wang,Yuanyuan Zhu,Xiao Yan,Jiawei Jiang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: PBKV系统包含两个核心模块：(1) 预测模块：融合历史工作流指导与目标工作流上下文，预测未来若干步的代理调用；(2) 缓存管理模块：基于预测评估缓存条目的复用潜力，将高潜力条目保留在GPU内存中。在缓存淘汰和预取时均采用保守策略以增强对预测误差的鲁棒性。

Result: 在三个工作流基准上，PBKV在动态工作流上相比LRU实现最高1.85倍加速，在静态工作流上相比SOTA基线KVFlow实现最高1.26倍加速。

Conclusion: PBKV通过预测驱动的KV缓存管理策略，有效解决了动态LLM工作流中的缓存复用问题，在兼顾鲁棒性的同时取得了显著的性能提升，验证了基于预测的缓存管理在动态工作流场景下的有效性。

Abstract: LLM-based workflows compose specialized agents to execute complex tasks, and these agents usually share substantial context, allowing KV-Cache reuse to save computation. Existing approaches either manage KV-Cache at agent level and fail to exploit the reuse opportunities within workflows, or manage cache at the workflow level but assume that each workflow calls a static sequence of agents. However, practical workflows are typically dynamic, where the sequence of invoked agents and thus induced cache reuse opportunities depend on the context of each task. To serve such dynamic workflows efficiently, we build a system dubbed PBKV (\textbf{P}rediction-\textbf{B}ased \textbf{KV}-Cache Management). For each workflow, PBKV predicts the agent invocations in several future steps by fusing the guidance from historical workflows and context of the target workflow. Based on the predictions, PBKV estimates the reuse potential of cache entries and keeps the high-potential entries in GPU memory. To be robust to prediction errors, PBKV utilizes the predictions conservatively during both cache eviction and prefetching. Experiments on three workflow benchmarks show that PBKV achieves up to $1.85\times$ speedup over LRU on dynamic workflows, and up to $1.26\times$ speedup over the SOTA baseline KVFlow on the static workflow.

### [199] [Operator-Guided Invariance Learning for Continuous Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06500)
*Zuyuan Zhang,Fei Xu Yu,Tian Lan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出VPSD-RL框架，通过Lie群作用与pullback算子发现连续强化学习中的值保持结构，并利用HJB残差最小化学习近似结构，提升数据效率与鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 连续时间/状态/动作空间的强化学习存在数据效率低、对干扰敏感的问题，现有方法仅考虑预设对称性与精确等变性，缺乏对更一般值保持结构的自动发现能力。

Method: 将连续RL建模为受控扩散，通过Lie群作用及其pullback算子定义值保持映射；证明值保持结构等价于值函数的pullback与动作的pushforward与受控生成元及奖励泛函可交换；当HJB残差较小时可找到带严格保证的近似结构；通过学习可微漂移/扩散/奖励模型，最小化确定方程残差学习无穷小生成元，经ODE流指数映射得到有限变换，并通过转移增广与变换一致性正则化集成到连续RL中。

Conclusion: VPSD-RL能够自动发现连续RL中的精确与近似值保持结构，为提升数据效率与鲁棒性提供了理论保证与实用方法。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) with continuous time and state/action spaces is often data-intensive and brittle under nuisance variability and shift, motivating methods that exploit value-preserving structures to stabilize and improve learning. Most existing approaches focus on special cases, such as prescribed symmetries and exact equivariance, without addressing how to discover more general structures that require nonlinear operators to transform and map between continuous state/action systems with isomorphic value functions. We propose \textbf{VPSD-RL} (Value-Preserving Structure Discovery for Reinforcement Learning). It models continuous RL as a controlled diffusion with value-preserving mappings defined through Lie-group actions and associated pullback operators. We show that a value-preserving structure exists exactly when pulling back the value function and pushing forward actions commute with the controlled generator and reward functional. Further, approximate value-preserving structures with rigorous guarantees can be found when the Hamilton--Jacobi--Bellman mismatch is small. This framework discovers exact and approximate value-preserving structures by searching for the associated Lie group operators. VPSD-RL fits differentiable drift, diffusion, and reward models; learns infinitesimal generators via determining-equation residual minimization; exponentiates them with ODE flows to obtain finite transformations; and integrates them into continuous RL through transition augmentation and transformation-consistency regularization. We show that bounded generator/reward mismatch implies quantitative stability of the optimal value function along approximate orbits, with sensitivity governed by the effective horizon, and observe improved data efficiency and robustness on continuous-control benchmarks.
